      2308 +      negative_words = ['çˆ›', 'çƒ‚', 'å·®', 'å»¢', 'åºŸ', 'æ²’ç”¨', 'æ²¡ç”¨', 'é¨™', 'éª—', 'å‡', 'åƒåœ¾',

      2345 +      for text, _, pub_time in comments:
      2346 +          if not text or not pub_time:
      2347 +              continue
      2348 +          month_match = re.search(r'(\d{4})-(\d{2})', str(pub_time))
      2349 +          if month_match:
      2350 +              month_key = f"{month_match.group(1)}-{month_match.group(2)}"
      2351 +              for topic, pattern in topics.items():
      2352 +                  if re.search(pattern, text):
      2353 +                      monthly_topics[month_key][topic] += 1
      2354 +
      2355 +      sorted_months = sorted(monthly_topics.keys())[-6:] if monthly_topics else []
      2356 +
      2357 +      trend_data = {
      2358 +          "months": sorted_months,
      2359 +          "topics": {}
      2360 +      }
      2361 +      for topic in topics:
      2362 +          trend_data["topics"][topic] = [monthly_topics[m].get(topic, 0) for m in sorted_months]
      2363 +
      2364 +      # ========== æ¨¡å¼42ï¼šé«˜èµè¯„è®ºç‰¹å¾ ==========
      2365 +      cursor.execute("""
      2366 +          SELECT text, like_count FROM video_comments
      2367 +          WHERE like_count > 0 AND text IS NOT NULL
      2368 +          ORDER BY like_count DESC LIMIT 100
      2369 +      """)
      2370 +      top_comments = cursor.fetchall()
      2371 +
      2372 +      if top_comments:
      2373 +          avg_len = sum(len(t[0]) for t in top_comments) / len(top_comments)
      2374 +          experience_words = ['æˆ‘', 'è‡ªå·±', 'è¦ªèº«', 'äº²èº«', 'è©¦é', 'è¯•è¿‡', 'ç¶“æ­·', 'ç»å†',

           + experience_words))
      2376 +          has_question = sum(1 for t in top_comments if '?' in t[0] or 'ï¼Ÿ' in t[0])
      2377 +
      2378 +          high_liked_data = {
      2379 +              "avg_length": round(avg_len),
      2380 +              "has_experience_pct": has_experience,
      2381 +              "has_question_pct": has_question,
      2382 +              "max_likes": top_comments[0][1] if top_comments else 0
